"In the third trimester , the amniotic fluid index ( AFI ) may be affected by maternal fluid status .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE

"From June 11 to August 16 , 1993 , during a period of unusual high heat , 42 women with singleton pregnancies between 27 and 40 weeks ' gestation undergoing serial antenatal testing had AFI determinations recorded at least weekly .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE

"A 2- , 3- , and 4-day mean temperature prior to the test date was compared to AFI using a Spearman-rank Correlation .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE

"There was a significant correlation between the 2- , 3- , and 4-day mean temperature and AFI , with the 4-day mean being the most significant ( r = 0.31 , p & # 60 ; 0.001 ) .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE

OBJECTIVE : To identify additional genetic risk factors for late-onset AD .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
DESIGN : A complete genomic screen was performed ( N=280 markers ) .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"Critical values for chromosomal regional follow-up were a P value of .05 or less for affected relative pair analysis or sibpair analysis , a parametric lod score of 1.0 or greater , or both .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE

SETTING : Clinic populations in the continental United States .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"PATIENTS : > From a series of multiplex families affected with late-onset ( > or =60 years ) AD ascertained during the last 14 years ( National Insititute of Neurological Disorders and Stroke-Alzheimer 's Disease and Related Disorders Association diagnostic criteria ) and for which DNA has been obtained , a subset of 16 families ( 135 total family members , 52 of whom were patients with AD ) was used for the genomic screen .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"A second subset of 38 families ( 216 total family members , 89 of whom were patients with AD ) was used for the follow-up analysis .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE

RESULTS : Fifteen chromosomal regions warranted initial follow-up .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"Follow-up analyses revealed 4 regions of continued interest on chromosomes 4 , 6 , 12 , and 20 , with the strongest results observed forchromosome 12 .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"Peak 2-point affecteds-only lod scores ( n=54 ) were 1.3 , 1.6 , 2.7 , and 2.2 and affected relative pairs P values ( n=54 ) were .04 , .03 , .14 , and .04 for D12S373 , D12S1057 , D12S1042 , and D12S390 , respectively .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"Sibpair analysis ( n=54 ) resulted in maximum lod scores ( MLSs ) of 1.5 , 2.6 , 3.2 , and 2.3 for these markers , with a peak multipoint MLS of 3.5 .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
A priori stratification by APOE genotype identified 27 families that had at least 1 member with AD whose genotype did not contain an APOE*4 allele .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE

Haplotype frequencies were estimated with standard maximum likelihood methods .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"RESULTS : The HLA effect is due to the class II DR2 haplotype , DRB1*1501-DQA1*0102-DRB1*0602 ; contributions to MS susceptibility from additional DRB1-DQB1 alleles or other HLA region loci were not observed .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE

"The distribution of haplotypes from 5 loci within the chromosome 19q13.2 region , including D19S178 , D19S574 , APOE , APOC2 , and D19S219 , differed between patient and control samples .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
D19S574 showed a significant effect ( P=.015 ) in Caucasian patients with MS due to the increased frequency of a single allele ( P=.002 ) .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"The APOE variation , prominent in other neurological diseases , showed no influence on MS susceptibility , despite its location within the chromosome 19q13.2 region .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE

"Current pharmacovigilance is predominantly based on spontaneous reporting and is mainly helpful in detecting type B effects ( those effects that are often allergic or idiosyncratic reactions , characteristically occurring in only a minority of patients and usually unrelated to dosage and that are serious , unexpected and unpredictable ) and unusual type A effects ( those effects that are related to the pharmacological effects of the drug and are dosage-related ) .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE

Molecular dynamics in torsion-angle space was applied to nuclear magnetic resonance structure calculation using nuclear Overhauser effect-derived distances and J-coupling-constant-derived dihedral angle restraints .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"Compared to two other commonly used algorithms , molecular dynamics in Cartesian space and metric-matrix geometry combined with Cartesian molecular dynamics , the method shows increased computational efficiency and success rate for large proteins , and it shows a dramatically increased radius of convergence for DNA .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"The torsion-angle molecular dynamics algorithm starts from an extended strand conformation and proceeds in four stages : high-temperature torsion-angle molecular dynamics , slow-cooling torsion-angle molecular dynamics , Cartesian molecular dynamics , and minimization .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"Tests were carried out using experimental NMR data for protein G , interleukin-8 , villin 14T , and a 12 base-pair duplex of DNA , and simulated NMR data for bovine pancreatic trypsin inhibitor .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"For villin 14T , a monomer consisting of 126 residues , structure determination by torsion-angle molecular dynamics has a success rate of 85 % , a more than twofold improvement over other methods .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"In the case of the 12 base-pair DNA duplex , torsion-angle molecular dynamics had a success rate of 52 % while Cartesian molecular dynamics and metric-matrix distance geometry always failed .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"The wavelet-transform method is used to quantify the magnetic resonance spectroscopy ( MRS ) parameters : chemical shift , apparent relaxation time T2 , resonance amplitude , and phase .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"Wavelet transformation is a time-frequency representation which separates each component from the FID , then successively quantifies it and subtracts it from the raw signal .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
Two iterative procedures have been developed .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"They have been combined with a nonlinear regression analysis method and tested on both simulated and real sets of biomedical MRS data selected with respect to the main problems usually encountered in quantifying biomedical MRS , specifically `` chemical noise , '' resulting from overlapping resonances , and baseline distortion .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
The results indicate that the wavelet-transform method can provide efficient and accurate quantification of MRS data .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
METHODS : We used a randomised double-blind study design .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE

The treatment was for 30 days .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE

"Many amino acids contain an asymmetric centre , occurring as laevorotatory , L , or dextrorotatory , D , compounds .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
It is generally assumed that abiotic synthesis of amino acids on the early Earth resulted in racemic mixtures ( L- and D-enantiomers in equal abundance ) .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"But the origin of life required , owing to conformational constraints , the almost exclusive selection of either L- or D-enantiomers , and the question of why living systems on the Earth consist of L-enantiomers rather than D-enantiomers is unresolved .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
A substantial fraction of the organic compounds on the early Earth may have been derived from comet and meteorite impacts .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"It has been reported previously that amino acids in the Murchison meteorite exhibit an excess of L-enantiomers , raising the possibility that a similar excess was present in the initial inventory of organic compounds on the Earth .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
The stable carbon isotope compositions of individual amino acids in Murchison support an extraterrestrial origin -- rather than a terrestrial overprint of biological amino acids-although reservations have persisted .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"Here we show that individual amino-acid enantiomers from Murchison are enriched in 15N relative to their terrestrial counterparts , so confirming an extraterrestrial source for an L-enantiomer excess in the Solar System that may predate the origin of life on the Earth .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE

"The effectiveness of treatment was assessed by conducting three measurements on each muscle before and immediately after treatment : subjective pain intensity ( ( PI ) with a visual analog scale ) , pressure pain threshold ( ( PT ) with algometry ) , and range of motion ( ( ROM ) with a goniometer ) of upper trapezius muscle ( lateral bending of cervical spine to the opposite side ) .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"When the effectiveness of treatment was compared with that of the placebo group ( group A ) , there was significant improvement in PI and PT in group B ( P & # 60 ; 0.01 ) but not in group C ( P > 0.05 ) .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
The improvement of ROM was significantly more in group C ( P & # 60 ; 0.01 ) as compared with that in group A or group B .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"When each group was divided into two additional subgroups based on the initial PI , it was found that ENS could reduce PI and increase PT significantly ( P & # 60 ; 0.05 ) , but did not significantly ( P > 0.05 ) improve ROM , as compared with the placebo group for both subgroups .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"EMS could significantly ( P & # 60 ; 0.05 ) improve ROM , but not PT , better than the placebo groups , for either subgroup .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"It could reduce PI significantly more ( P & # 60 ; 0.05 ) than placebo controls only for the subgroup with mild to moderate pain , but not with severe pain .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE

CONTEXT : Adolescents ' concerns about privacy in clinical settings decrease their willingness to seek health care for sensitive problems and may inhibit their communication with physicians .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
OBJECTIVE : To investigate the influence of physicians ' assurances of confidentiality on adolescents ' willingness to disclose information and seek future health care .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
DESIGN : Randomized controlled trial .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
SETTING : Three suburban public high schools in California .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
PARTICIPANTS : The 562 participating adolescents represented 92 % of students in mandatory classes .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"INTERVENTION : After random assignment to 1 of 3 groups , the adolescents listened to a standardized audiotape depiction of an office visit during which they heard a physician who assured unconditional confidentiality , a physician who assured conditional confidentiality , or a physician who did not mention confidentiality .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"MAIN OUTCOME MEASURES : Adolescents ' willingness to disclose general information , willingness to disclose information about sensitive topics , intended honesty , and likelihood of return visits to the physician depicted in the scenario were assessed by anonymous written questionnaire .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"RESULTS : Assurances of confidentiality increased the number of adolescents willing to disclose sensitive information about sexuality , substance use , and mental health from 39 % ( 68/175 ) to 46.5 % ( 178/383 ) ( beta=.10 , P=.02 ) and increased the number willing to seek future health care from 53 % ( 93/175 ) to 67 % ( 259/386 ) ( beta=.17 , P & # 60 ; .001 ) .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"When comparing the unconditional with the conditional groups , assurances of unconditional confidentiality increased the number of adolescents willing to return for a future visit by 10 percentage points , from 62 % ( 122/196 ) to 72 % ( 137/190 ) ( beta=.14 , P=.001 ) .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
CONCLUSIONS : Adolescents are more willing to communicate with and seek health care from physicians who assure confidentiality .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
Further investigation is needed to identify a confidentiality assurance statement that explains the legal and ethical limitations of confidentiality without decreasing adolescents ' likelihood of seeking future health care for routine and nonreportable sensitive health concerns .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
Granulocyte-colony stimulating factor ( G-CSF ) increases the release of neutrophils from the bone marrow and improves neutrophil function .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE

The fast reaction of peroxynitrite with CO2 and the high concentration of dissolved CO2 in vivo ( ca .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
1 mM ) suggest that CO2 modulates most of the reactions of peroxynitrite in biological systems .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
The addition of peroxynitrite to CO2 produces of the adduct ONOO-CO2- ( 1 ) .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
The production of 1 greatly accelerates the decomposition of peroxynitrite to give nitrate .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
We now show that the formation of 1 is followed by reformation of CO2 ( rather than another carbonate species such as CO3 = or HCO3- ) .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"To show this , it is necessary to study systems with limiting concentrations of CO2 .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"( When CO2 is present in excess , its concentration remains nearly constant during the decomposition of peroxynitrite , and the recycling of CO2 , although it occurs , can not be detected kinetically ) .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE

"Switch substrate retrovectors ( SSR ) contain a long-terminal repeat-driven neomycin ( Neo ) gene for proviral chromosomal maintenance ( pre- and post-S recombination ) and a CMV promoter-driven , chimeric hygromycin-thymidine kinase ( Hytk ) gene ( flanked by S mu and S gamma 2b recombination targets ) to select for ( ganciclovir ) and against ( hygromycin B ) S region recombination .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"The retro-substrates ' strong , constitutive promoters ensure that variations in cellular switch recombinase activities are independent of S region accessibility control .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"By initially selecting for proviral integrants in hygromycin followed by shifting into neomycin + ganciclovir to select for S sequence-mediated deletions , switch recombinations can be specifically forestalled in B cell lines whilst most switch-incompetent cells do not survive secondary selection .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"A qualitative , direct PCR assay reveals that SSR recombinations are stochastic in B cell lines generating a product array akin to natural GH class switching .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
A semi-quantitative DC-PCR assay detects a significant recombinase activity only in a restricted set of late stage pre-B and mature B cell lines .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
BCL1B1 mature B cells have the highest level of recombinase activity with 25 % or more of proviral integrants accumulating S mu/S gamma 2b substrate recombinations within 10-14 cell generations .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"The SSR recombinase assay can be performed in a transient fashion wherein extensive , B cell-specific recombination can be visualized within only a few cell divisions post proviral integration .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
We propose that switch recombinase activity becomes activated during B cell ontogeny independent of or prior to the acquisition of CH locus accessibility and that endogenous S segment targeting to pre-existing recombinase requires a level of accessibility beyond transcriptional activation .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE

OBJECTIVES : The purpose of this descriptive exploratory study was to examine critical care nurses ' responses to three questions about health practices in their daily lives : ( 1 ) What are critical care nurses doing currently to stay healthy ? METHODS : One hundred twenty-seven critical care nurses attending a midwestern critical care conference completed a two-part questionnaire designed to produce a health profile .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE

"For example , for the binding of 10 nM insulin growth factor-1 in solution to insulin growth factor binding protein-1 immobilized on a biosensor surface , a 64 % increase in the fractal dimension from 1.73 ( Df1 ) to 2.85 ( Df2 ) leads to an increase in the binding rate coefficient by a factor of 31.8 from 3.92 ( k1 ) to 125 ( k2 ) .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"Furthermore , as the IGF-1 concentration in solution increases from 10 to 80 nM in solution , k2 and Df2 exhibit a linear increase .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE

"Also , the magnitude of the changes in the binding rate coefficients ( k1 and k2 ) and in the fractal dimensions ( Df1 and Df2 ) as different parameters are changed for the different biosensor applications are of particular value , since they provide us with a measure or extent of changes in the binding rate coefficient on changing different experimental parameter values .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE

"The search of solutions needs multiple competences from the physician , who has to play an essential role .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
Dioxins are a family of chlorinated aromatic hydrocarbons that are produced during combustion processes in the presence of a chlorine donor and as by-products of the chlorine-processing chemical industries .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
Several dioxins are extremely stable compounds and persist for years in the environment .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
Exposure to dioxins occurs mainly via the ingestion of contaminated food .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
The lipophilic character of dioxins prevents their excretion in the urine and causes their accumulation in body fat .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
The mechanisms of dioxin action are similar to those of a hormone .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
Dioxins bind to a specific intracellular receptor and the complex acts as a transcription factor that induces the production of a great number of proteins .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"Certain dioxins , particularly 2 , 3 , 7 , 8-tetrachlorodibenzo-p-dioxin , are very toxic and able to induce numerous clinical conditions .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
The carcinogenicity of dioxins is well documented in animal models and has been described in humans after professional and accidental exposures .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
The particular sensibility of the fetus and newborn is of concern because the exposition to dioxins is particularly important during those periods of life .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
The chronological parallelism with the appearance of dioxins in the environment suggests that these might exert biological effects at the prevailing level of exposure .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
Nevertheless this hypothesis is currently unconfirmed by epidemiological studies .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
The implications of this scientific incertitude for the implementation of preventive measures are briefly discussed .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
This presentation summarizes the debate on the suggested progressive impairment of semen quality ( the `` sperm fall '' ) in the last forty years in the developed countries .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"The various available data strongly suggesting an environmental toxic origin for the `` sperm fall '' will be presented as well as the most frequently suspected class of substances , the xenoestrogens .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"These last drugs seem very attractive because they decrease insulin resistance in obese , diabetics .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
Their hepatic side effects must be however under control .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"The advances in the understanding of the neuro-hormonal mechanisms of heart failure have modified the therapeutic strategy : the deleterious effect of the activation of the sympathetic nervous system on the myocardium has served as the rationale for randomized clinical trials comparing beta-blockade to placebo : the current data are promising , suggesting a beneficial effect on survival as well as on quality of life .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"However , these results have to be confirmed by larger trials , currently underway , before to consider that beta-blockade should definitely be incorporated in the treatment of heart failure .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"Randomized prospective studies have , however , never been able to confirm these observations .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"These drugs are very efficacious and generally devoided of important side effects , but they are expensive and therefore have to be compared with other , more conventional drugs with established or assumed efficacy .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
Fiercer competition between athletes and a wider knowledge of optimal training regimens dramatically influence current training methods .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"A single training bout per day was previously considered sufficient , whereas today athletes regularly train twice a day or more .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"Consequently , the number of athletes who are overtraining and have insufficient rest is increasing .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
Positive overtraining can be regarded as a natural process when the end result is adaptation and improved performance : the supercompensation principle -- which includes the breakdown process ( training ) followed by the recovery process ( rest ) -- is well known in sports .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"However , negative overtraining , causing maladaptation and other negative consequences such as staleness , can occur .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"Physiological , psychological , biochemical and immunological symptoms must be considered , both independently and together , to fully understand the 'staleness ' syndrome .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"However , psychological testing may reveal early-warning signs more readily than the various physiological or immunological markers .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
The time frame of training and recovery is also important since the consequences of negative overtraining comprise an overtraining-response continuum from short to long term effects .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
An athlete failing to recover within 72 hours has presumably negatively overtrained and is in an overreached state .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"For an elite athlete to refrain from training for > 72 hours is extremely undesirable , highlighting the importance of a carefully monitored recovery process .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
There are many methods used to measure the training process but few with which to match the recovery process against it .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
One such framework for this is referred to as the total quality recovery ( TQR ) process .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"By using a TQR scale , structured around the scale developed for ratings of perceived exertion ( RPE ) , the recovery process can be monitored and matched against the breakdown ( training ) process ( TQR versus RPE ) .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
The TQR scale emphasises both the athlete 's perception of recovery and the importance of active measures to improve the recovery process .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"Furthermore , directing attention to psychophysiological cues serves the same purpose as in RPE , i.e. increasing self-awareness .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
This article reviews and conceptualises the whole overtraining process .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"In doing so , it ( i ) aims to differentiate between the types of stress affecting an athlete 's performance : ( ii ) identifies factors influencing an athlete 's ability to adapt to physical training : ( iii ) structures the recovery process .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
The TQR method to facilitate monitoring of the recovery process is then suggested and a conceptual model that incorporates all of the important parameters for performance gain ( adaptation ) and loss ( maladaptation ) .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
Little attention has been directed toward identifying the changes which occur in salivary composition in response to exercise .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"To address this , our article first refers to the main aspects of salivary gland physiology .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
A knowledge of the neural control of salivary secretion is especially important for the understanding of the effects of exertion on salivary secretion .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
Both salivary output and composition depend on the activity of the autonomic nervous system and any modification of this activity can be observed indirectly by alternations in the salivary excretion .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"The effects of physical activity ( with reference to factors such as exercise intensity and duration , or type of exercise protocol ) on salivary composition are then considered .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"Exercise might indeed induce changes in several salivary components such as immunoglobulins , hormones , lactate , proteins and electrolytes .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
Saliva composition might therefore be used as an alternative noninvasive indicator of the response of the different body tissues and systems to physical exertion .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"In this respect , the response of salivary amylase and salivary electrolytes to incremental levels of exercise is of particular interest .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"Beyond a certain intensity of exercise , and coinciding with the accumulation of blood lactate ( anaerobic threshold or AT ) , a 'saliva threshold ' ( Tsa ) does indeed exist .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
Tsa is the point during exercise at which the levels of salivary alpha-amylase and electrolytes ( especially Na+ ) also begin to rise above baseline levels .,"['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"The occurrence of the 2 thresholds ( AT and Tsa ) might , in turn , be attributable to the same underlying mechanism , that of increased adrenal sympathetic activity at high exercise intensities .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"Fat is an extremely important substrate for muscle contraction , both at rest and during exercise .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"Triglycerides ( TGs ) , stored in adipose tissue and within muscle fibres , are considered to be the main source of the free fatty acids ( FFAs ) oxidised during exercise .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"It is still unclear , however , how the use of these substrates is regulated during exercise .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"The regulation seems to be multifactorial and includes : ( i ) dietary and nutritional status ; ( ii ) hormonal milieu ; ( iii ) exercise mode , intensity and duration ; and ( iv ) training status .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"On the other hand , the mechanism for FFA transport from its storage as triglycerides in adipose tissue and muscle to its place of utilisation in heart , skeletal muscle , kidney and liver is more clearly understood .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE

"However , an exercise intensity of 65 % VO2max results in a slight decrease in the amount of plasma FFA uptake by muscle tissue .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"Other studies have found that during prolonged exercise , muscle TGs become the predominant source of energy obtained from fat .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"Furthermore , it is widely documented that endurance activities increase the energy utilisation from fat while sparing carbohydrate sources .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"For example , during exercise on a cycle ergometer , nonplasma FFAs and plasma FFAs contribute 40 % , and carbohydrates 60 % , of the total calculated amount of energy expenditure before exercise and vice versa after exercise ( 60 % nonplasma and plasma FFAs and 40 % carbohydrates ) .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"Although it was many years before it was fully demonstrated , fat is now known to be transported in the blood as FFA bound to the protein carrier albumin .","['O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O', 'O']",NONE
"The mobilisation of FFA is primarily a function of sympathetic nervous activity directed towards the adipocytes , or the 'fat pad'.
